Task theunitedkingdom

//instantiating the map canvas
//THIS CALLS THE MAPCANVAS MODULE WHICH FUNNELS THIS INFORMATION ON TO
//THE MAIN PROGRAM

Call mapcanvas @

//variables used by this module
//THESE VARIABLES ARE USED TO CONVEY THE GEOGRAPHIC INFORMATION FROM
//THIS MODULE THROUGH THE MAPCANVAS TO THE MAIN PROGRAM
Common Int polyarray[1000]
Common Int coords
Common Float2 x[10000]
Common Float2 y[10000]
Common Float2 z[10000]
Common Float2 scale[2]
Common Float2 roll
Common Float2 pitch
Common Float2 yaw

//these set values for scaling and rotation of the image
//THESE VALUES ARE OPTIONAL AND NEED NOT BE A PART OF THE FILE, BUT
//SET DEFAULT POSITIONING INFORMATION FOR THE POLYGONS
Set scale[0] = .75
Set scale[1] = .75

Set roll = 240
Set pitch = 20
Set yaw = 270

//this is the geographic information for this coverage
//THE POLYARRAY VARIABLE ARRAY ENTRIES INDICATE HOW MANY POINTS ARE IN

//ALTITUDE, RESPECTIVELY) ARE SET.  (A SEPARATE PROGRAM, CALLED
//"POLYCREATE", CAN CONSTRUCT THIS FROM A CSV DATA FILE WHERE THE
//NUMBERS ARE MERELY LISTED IN ORDER, WITHOUT THE "SET" COMMANDS.
